### (10) Mistake Group ['R.1.0', 'R.1.1'] of size 10
""" Please write hint here """

|ID	|Author	|Condition	|Hint Text|
|---|---|---|---|
|0|	|['R.1.0', 'R.1.1']	|"hint"	|

|	|Answer	|Attempt	|Matching sub-exp|
|---|---|---|---|
|0	|0+0+1/3	|0+0+1/3	|[('R.1.0', 1.0, '1', u'1'), ('R.1.1', 3.0, '3', u'3')]	|
|1	|0+0+1/3	|0+0+(1/3)	|[('R.1.0', 1.0, '1', u'1'), ('R.1.1', 3.0, '3', u'3')]	|
|2	|0+0+1/3	|0 + 0 + 1/3	|[('R.1.0', 1.0, '1', u'1'), ('R.1.1', 3.0, '3', u'3')]	|

""" Please write hint here """

|0|	|['R.1.0', 'R.1.1']	|"hint"	|

|	|Answer	|Attempt	|Matching sub-exp|
|---|---|---|---|
|0	|0+0+1/3	|0+0+1/3	|[('R.1.0', 1.0, '1', u'1'), ('R.1.1', 3.0, '3', u'3')]	|
|1	|0+0+1/3	|0+0+(1/3)	|[('R.1.0', 1.0, '1', u'1'), ('R.1.1', 3.0, '3', u'3')]	|
|2	|0+0+1/3	|0 + 0 + 1/3	|[('R.1.0', 1.0, '1', u'1'), ('R.1.1', 3.0, '3', u'3')]	|
